### 3.2 å·¥ä½œäººå‘˜è¯†åˆ«å’Œä»‹å…¥åˆ¤æ–­é€»è¾‘æ··ä¹± âŒ

**1. å·¥ä½œäººå‘˜è¯†åˆ«ç­–ç•¥**

```javascript
// è¯†åˆ«å·¥ä½œäººå‘˜
function identifyStaffUser(user) {
  // 1. æ£€æŸ¥ä¼ä¸šåç§°ï¼ˆä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡ç”¨æˆ·ï¼‰
  if (user.enterpriseName) {
    // æ£€æŸ¥ç”¨æˆ·IDæ˜¯å¦åœ¨å·¥ä½œäººå‘˜åˆ—è¡¨ä¸­
    const staffUser = staffUsers.find(s => s.userId === user.userId);
    if (staffUser) {
      return {
        isStaff: true,
        staffType: staffUser.type, // 'after_sales' | 'assistant' | 'admin'
        staffUserId: staffUser.userId,
        staffName: staffUser.name
      };
    }
  }

  // 2. æ£€æŸ¥æ˜µç§°åŒ¹é…ï¼ˆå¾®ä¿¡ç”¨æˆ·ï¼‰
  const staffByNickname = staffUsers.find(s => s.nickname === user.userName);
  if (staffByNickname) {
    return {
      isStaff: true,
      staffType: staffByNickname.type,
      staffUserId: staffByNickname.userId,
      staffName: staffByNickname.name
    };
  }

  return { isStaff: false };
}
```

**2. å·¥ä½œäººå‘˜æ¶ˆæ¯å¤„ç†é€»è¾‘**
```
å·¥ä½œäººå‘˜æ¶ˆæ¯ â†’ è®°å½•å·¥ä½œäººå‘˜æ´»åŠ¨ â†’ åˆ¤æ–­æ¶ˆæ¯ç±»å‹
  â”œâ”€ å›å¤ç”¨æˆ· â†’ æ£€æŸ¥å›å¤è´¨é‡ â†’ å¦‚æœè´¨é‡å·®ï¼Œè§¦å‘ä»‹å…¥æé†’
  â”œâ”€ @ç”¨æˆ· â†’ è®°å½•@è¡Œä¸º â†’ æ£€æŸ¥ç”¨æˆ·æ˜¯å¦å“åº” â†’ è®¾ç½®è¶…æ—¶å‘Šè­¦
  â”œâ”€ è¯¢é—®å·ä¸» â†’ è®°å½•è¯¢é—® â†’ ç­‰å¾…ç”¨æˆ·å›å¤
  â””â”€ å…¶ä»– â†’ åªè®°å½•ï¼Œä¸å¤„ç†
```

**3. ä»‹å…¥åˆ¤æ–­é€»è¾‘ï¼ˆè¯¦ç»†ï¼‰**
```javascript
// ä»‹å…¥åˆ¤æ–­
function shouldIntervene(context, senderType, messageType) {
  // æƒ…å†µ1ï¼šç”¨æˆ·å›å¤å·¥ä½œäººå‘˜
  if (senderType === 'user' && context.lastSenderType === 'staff') {
    // æ£€æŸ¥ç”¨æˆ·å›å¤å†…å®¹
    if (isNegativeResponse(context.lastUserMessage)) {
      return {
        shouldIntervene: true,
        reason: 'user_negative_response_to_staff',
        priority: 'high'
      };
    }

    // æ£€æŸ¥ç”¨æˆ·ç­‰å¾…æ—¶é—´
    const waitTime = Date.now() - context.lastStaffMessageTime;
    if (waitTime > 30 * 60 * 1000) { // 30åˆ†é’Ÿ
      return {
        shouldIntervene: true,
        reason: 'user_waiting_too_long',
        priority: 'medium'
      };
    }
  }

  // æƒ…å†µ2ï¼šå·¥ä½œäººå‘˜å›å¤è´¨é‡å·®
  if (senderType === 'staff') {
    const replyQuality = analyzeReplyQuality(context.currentMessage);
    if (replyQuality < 0.5) { // è´¨é‡ä½äº50%
      return {
        shouldIntervene: true,
        reason: 'staff_low_reply_quality',
        priority: 'high',
        suggestion: generateSuggestion(context.currentMessage)
      };
    }
  }

  // æƒ…å†µ3ï¼šç”¨æˆ·æ»¡æ„åº¦ä½
  if (context.userSatisfaction < 0.3) {
    return {
      shouldIntervene: true,
      reason: 'low_user_satisfaction',
      priority: 'urgent'
    };
  }

  // æƒ…å†µ4ï¼šæ¶ˆæ¯ç±»å‹éœ€è¦ä»‹å…¥
  if (messageType === 'user_complaint') {
    return {
      shouldIntervene: true,
      reason: 'user_complaint',
      priority: 'urgent'
    };
  }

  return { shouldIntervene: false };
}
```

## 8. å”®åæœåŠ¡æµç¨‹è®¾è®¡

### 8.1 å”®åä»»åŠ¡ç±»å‹

| ä»»åŠ¡ç±»å‹ | æè¿° | ä¼˜å…ˆçº§ | å¹³å‡å¤„ç†æ—¶é—´ | å¤æ‚åº¦ |
|---------|------|-------|-------------|--------|
| æ‰«ç è§†é¢‘è®¤è¯ | éœ€è¦å·ä¸»æ‰«ç è¿›è¡Œè§†é¢‘è®¤è¯ï¼ˆ60-70%ï¼‰ | high | 10-30åˆ†é’Ÿ | ä¸­ç­‰ |
| ç»‘å®šæ‰‹æœºå· | å·ä¸»è§†é¢‘å·æ²¡æœ‰ç»‘æ‰‹æœºå· | normal | 5-10åˆ†é’Ÿ | ç®€å• |
| å®åè®¤è¯ | å·ä¸»å®åæ‰äº†éœ€è¦é‡æ–°è®¤è¯ | high | 15-30åˆ†é’Ÿ | ä¸­ç­‰ |
| å‘è‡ªæ‹è§†é¢‘ | éœ€è¦å·ä¸»å‘10æ¡è‡ªæ‹è§†é¢‘è¿›è¡Œç”³è¯‰ | normal | 20-40åˆ†é’Ÿ | å¤æ‚ |
| ç§è‡ªæ·»åŠ å•†å“ | å·ä¸»ç§è‡ªæ·»åŠ å•†å“ï¼ˆç¦æ­¢ï¼‰ | urgent | 5-15åˆ†é’Ÿ | ç®€å• |
| åˆ é™¤ä½œå“ | å·ä¸»ç§è‡ªåˆ é™¤ä½œå“ï¼ˆç¦æ­¢ï¼‰ | urgent | 5-15åˆ†é’Ÿ | ç®€å• |
| è‡ªå·±å‘å¸ƒä½œå“ | å·ä¸»è‡ªå·±å‘å¸ƒä½œå“ï¼ˆç¦æ­¢ï¼‰ | urgent | 5-15åˆ†é’Ÿ | ç®€å• |
| å…¶ä»–å”®åéœ€æ±‚ | å…¶ä»–å”®åç›¸å…³é—®é¢˜ | normal | 10-30åˆ†é’Ÿ | ä¸å®š |

### 8.2 å”®åä»»åŠ¡è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ†é…ç­–ç•¥

```javascript
// å”®åä»»åŠ¡åˆ†é…è§„åˆ™
function assignAfterSalesTask(task: AfterSalesTask): StaffUser {
  // 1. è·å–æ‰€æœ‰åœ¨çº¿çš„å”®åäººå‘˜
  const onlineStaff = getOnlineStaffUsers('after_sales');

  // 2. æ ¹æ®å·¥ä½œè´Ÿè½½ç­›é€‰ï¼ˆå½“å‰ä»»åŠ¡æ•° < æœ€å¤§ä»»åŠ¡æ•°ï¼‰
  const availableStaff = onlineStaff.filter(staff =>
    staff.currentTasks < staff.maxTasks
  );

  if (availableStaff.length === 0) {
    // å¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰å¯ç”¨äººå‘˜ï¼Œåˆ†é…ç»™ä»»åŠ¡æ•°æœ€å°‘çš„äººå‘˜
    return onlineStaff.sort((a, b) => a.currentTasks - b.currentTasks)[0];
  }

  // 3. æ ¹æ®æŠ€èƒ½åŒ¹é…ç­›é€‰ï¼ˆä»»åŠ¡ç±»å‹ä¸äººå‘˜æŠ€èƒ½åŒ¹é…ï¼‰
  const matchedStaff = availableStaff.filter(staff =>
    staff.skills.includes(task.taskType)
  );

  if (matchedStaff.length === 0) {
    // å¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰æŠ€èƒ½åŒ¹é…ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨è½®è¯¢åˆ†é…
    return assignByRoundRobin(availableStaff);
  }

  // 4. ä¼˜å…ˆåˆ†é…ç»™ä»»åŠ¡æ•°å°‘çš„äººå‘˜
  return matchedStaff.sort((a, b) => a.currentTasks - b.currentTasks)[0];
}

// è½®è¯¢åˆ†é…
function assignByRoundRobin(staffList: StaffUser[]): StaffUser {
  // è®°å½•ä¸Šæ¬¡åˆ†é…çš„ç´¢å¼•
  const lastAssignIndex = getLastAssignIndex();
  const nextIndex = (lastAssignIndex + 1) % staffList.length;
  setLastAssignIndex(nextIndex);
  return staffList[nextIndex];
}
```

### 8.3 å”®åå®æ—¶ç›‘æ§å¤§å±è®¾è®¡

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
```

### 8.4 ç”¨æˆ·å“åº”ç›‘æ§

```javascript
// ç”¨æˆ·å“åº”ç›‘æ§é€»è¾‘
function monitorUserResponse(task: AfterSalesTask) {
  // 1. æ£€æµ‹ç”¨æˆ·æ˜¯å¦è¯´"åœ¨"
  const userMessages = getRecentUserMessages(task.sessionId, 5); // æœ€è¿‘5æ¡
  const onlineResponse = userMessages.find(msg =>
    msg.content.includes('åœ¨') || msg.content.includes('å¥½çš„') || msg.content.includes('æ”¶åˆ°')
  );

  if (onlineResponse) {
    // ç”¨æˆ·å“åº”äº†
    task.userResponseStatus = 'responded';
    task.userResponseTime = onlineResponse.timestamp;

    // ç¬¬ä¸€æ—¶é—´æé†’å”®åäººå‘˜
    sendUrgentNotificationToStaff({
      staffUserId: task.assignedStaffUserId,
      message: `ã€ç´§æ€¥ã€‘${task.groupName} ${task.userName}è¯´"${onlineResponse.content}"ï¼Œè¯·ç«‹å³å¤„ç†ï¼`,
      priority: 'urgent'
    });

    // åœ¨ç›‘æ§å¤§å±é«˜äº®æ˜¾ç¤º
    highlightTaskOnDashboard(task.id);
  }

  // 2. æ£€æµ‹ç”¨æˆ·æ˜¯å¦æ‹’ç»é…åˆ
  const refusalResponse = userMessages.find(msg =>
    msg.content.includes('ä¸') || msg.content.includes('æ²¡æ—¶é—´') || msg.content.includes('ä¸æƒ³')
  );

  if (refusalResponse) {
    // ç”¨æˆ·æ‹’ç»é…åˆ
    task.userResponseStatus = 'refused';
    task.userCooperationLevel = 'low';

    // è®°å½•é—®é¢˜
    recordCooperationIssue({
      userId: task.userId,
      userName: task.userName,
      issue: 'æ‹’ç»é…åˆ',
      reason: refusalResponse.content
    });
  }

  // 3. æ£€æµ‹è¶…æ—¶æœªå“åº”
  const timeSinceAt = Date.now() - task.staffAtUserTime;
  if (timeSinceAt > 30 * 60 * 1000) { // 30åˆ†é’Ÿ
    // ç”¨æˆ·æœªå“åº”ï¼Œæé†’å”®åäººå‘˜è·Ÿè¿›
    sendNotificationToStaff({
      staffUserId: task.assignedStaffUserId,
      message: `ã€æé†’ã€‘${task.groupName} ${task.userName}è¶…è¿‡30åˆ†é’Ÿæœªå“åº”ï¼Œè¯·è·Ÿè¿›ï¼`,
      priority: 'high'
    });
  }
}
```
